    USER: Are there any strict grammar mistakes in my sentence 'No one can forgive that comment to you.'? Answer like 'Yes,' or 'No,'. Start your respose with 'Yes' or 'No'
    ASSISTANT:
     Yes, I think there is a mistake in the phrase "to you" at the end of the sentence. The word "to" should be changed to "with." Here's why:
        When we use the preposition "to," it typically indicates direction or destination (e.g., "I threw the ball to John"). In this case, however, we are talking about someone forgiving a comment, which doesn't involve movement or direction. Instead, we should use the preposition "with" to indicate that the person is forgiving the comment together with the speaker.
     So, the corrected sentence would be: "No one can forgive that comment with you."
